Again, `log` but no `sin`.

None of these candidates contain a `sin` function. The GT has `sin(log(A+1))` which cannot be expressed as any combination of polynomials, exponentials, logarithms, or rational functions of A.

The function `sin(log(A+1))` is an oscillatory function that cannot be represented by any finite combination of the elementary functions present in these candidates (polynomials, exponentials, logarithms, rational functions, fractional powers).

Since `sin(log(A+1))` has infinitely many zeros (at `A = exp(nπ) - 1` for integer n) while all candidate expressions involve functions that have at most finitely many zeros (or are monotonic combinations), no candidate can exactly match the GT.

Let me double-check: could the coefficient of `sin(log(A+1))` be zero? Looking at the GT: `c3*_t = 0.11847 * 7.14436 = 0.84638`, which is nonzero. So the `sin` term is definitely present and nonzero.

Therefore, no candidate can match the GT, as none contain `sin` (or any oscillatory function).
